<time>1614876334001< /time><Rating>2<//Rating><text>Customer service, including dealing with the supervisor, was very disappointing.  I got the feeling that since the market is good and the homes  are in demand, they don't really feel a need to work for the customer.

The neighborhood is very nice and we enjoy the location, feel, and amenities.

The quality of the construction is not good.  Due to our timetable, we were not able to select any upgrades.  The base features for these homes is very basic.  The quality of the materials that are included in the base are the cheapest and poorest quality I've seen, especially in a house that is not exactly "low end".  The carpet is the cheapest version I believe you can get .  Show stains and already shows sign of wear within the first month.  The online site for requesting services for repairs seems great in theory, until you make a request and get no response for over a month.  Again, you get the feeling that once they have your money, you don't matter and if they drag out the repairs long enough the 1 year window will expire.

Be very wary of these homes.  Perhaps if you are able to choose your own upgrades you'll have better luck, but if you get what is included, be prepared to spend more money to replace everything to a higher quality on your own.< /text>< pics>

This B & R is consistent. Their ice cream, drinks and creations have always been really good, and the owner and his employees are long term which i believe is a positive sign. Happy employees = superior service.
I'm mostly a fan of their shakes (i ask for them without any added syrup, because they already sweet enough!) or just basic dishes or, cones, with their delicious flavors. Open every night, rain or shine until 10pm & they graciously accept those of us dashing in at the last minute:)
The ONLY drawback, at certain times during the day is the smallish parking lot...currently that isn't too terrible, though, because the party store adjacent to B & R, sadly closed, thus freeing up more parking. (For now!)<//Text>
